}</script><script>// Vanlife Trip Budget Simulator
(function () {
  function initVanlifeTripBudgetApp() {
    var app = document.getElementById("vanlife-trip-budget-app");
    if (!app) return;

    function q(selector) {
      return app.querySelector(selector);
    }

    var els = {
      vanType: q("[data-vl-van-type]"),
      distance: q("[data-vl-distance]"),
      mpg: q("[data-vl-mpg]"),
      gas: q("[data-vl-gas]"),
      nights: q("[data-vl-nights]"),
      campStyle: q("[data-vl-camp-style]"),
      foodStyle: q("[data-vl-food-style]"),
      misc: q("[data-vl-misc]"),

      distVal: q("[data-vl-distance-value]"),
      mpgVal: q("[data-vl-mpg-value]"),
      gasVal: q("[data-vl-gas-value]"),
      nightsVal: q("[data-vl-nights-value]"),
      miscVal: q("[data-vl-misc-value]"),

      total: q("[data-vl-total]"),
      daily: q("[data-vl-daily]"),
      weekly: q("[data-vl-weekly]"),
      weeklyNote: q("[data-vl-weekly-note]"),
      breakdown: q("[data-vl-breakdown]")
    };

    var presetButtons = app.querySelectorAll("[data-vl-preset]");

    function toNumber(val, fallback) {
      var n = parseFloat(val);
      return isNaN(n) ? (fallback || 0) : n;
    }

    function update() {
      var dist = toNumber(els.distance.value, 0);
      var mpg = toNumber(els.mpg.value, 1);
      var gas = toNumber(els.gas.value, 0);
      var nights = toNumber(els.nights.value, 1);
      if (nights <= 0) nights = 1;

      var camp = toNumber(els.campStyle.value, 0);
      var food = toNumber(els.foodStyle.value, 0);
      var misc = toNumber(els.misc.value, 0);

      // Update displayed values
      if (els.distVal) els.distVal.textContent = dist;
      if (els.mpgVal) els.mpgVal.textContent = mpg;
      if (els.gasVal) els.gasVal.textContent = "$" + gas.toFixed(2);
      if (els.nightsVal) els.nightsVal.textContent = nights;
      if (els.miscVal) els.miscVal.textContent = "$" + misc;

      // Core math
      var fuelCost = (dist / mpg) * gas;
      var campingCost = nights * camp;
      var foodCost = nights * food;
      var miscCost = nights * misc;

      var total = fuelCost + campingCost + foodCost + miscCost;
      var daily = total / nights;
      var weekly;

      // Weekly logic
      if (nights >= 7) {
        weekly = daily * 7;
        if (els.weeklyNote) {
          els.weeklyNote.textContent = "Weekly based on a full 7 days.";
        }
      } else {
        weekly = total;
        if (els.weeklyNote) {
          els.weeklyNote.textContent = "Weekly matches your trip total (shorter than 7 nights).";
        }
      }

      // Update totals
      if (els.total) els.total.textContent = "$" + Math.round(total);
      if (els.daily) els.daily.textContent = "Daily: $" + Math.round(daily);
      if (els.weekly) els.weekly.textContent = "Weekly: $" + Math.round(weekly);

      // Breakdown percentages
      if (els.breakdown) {
        if (total > 0) {
          var fuelPct = Math.round((fuelCost / total) * 100);
          var campPct = Math.round((campingCost / total) * 100);
          var foodPct = Math.round((foodCost / total) * 100);
          var miscPct = Math.max(0, 100 - fuelPct - campPct - foodPct); // fix rounding drift

          els.breakdown.textContent =
            "Fuel " + fuelPct + "% · Food " + foodPct + "% · Camping " + campPct + "% · Misc " + miscPct + "%";
        } else {
          els.breakdown.textContent = "Fuel 0% · Food 0% · Camping 0% · Misc 0%";
        }
      }
    }

    // Presets
    function applyPreset(name) {
      if (!els.distance || !els.mpg || !els.gas || !els.nights || !els.campStyle || !els.foodStyle || !els.misc) {
        return;
      }

      if (name === "weekend") {
        // ~2-night weekend test
        els.distance.value = 300;
        els.nights.value = 2;
        els.gas.value = 3.60;
        els.campStyle.value = "15";
        els.foodStyle.value = "22";
        els.misc.value = 8;
        if (els.vanType) {
          els.vanType.value = "22";
          els.mpg.value = "22";
        }
      } else if (name === "oneweek") {
        // ~7-night park loop
        els.distance.value = 800;
        els.nights.value = 7;
        els.gas.value = 3.60;
        els.campStyle.value = "15";
        els.foodStyle.value = "22";
        els.misc.value = 10;
        if (els.vanType) {
          els.vanType.value = "22";
          els.mpg.value = "22";
        }
      } else if (name === "twoweek") {
        // ~14-night long run
        els.distance.value = 1600;
        els.nights.value = 14;
        els.gas.value = 3.80;
        els.campStyle.value = "28";
        els.foodStyle.value = "22";
        els.misc.value = 12;
        if (els.vanType) {
          els.vanType.value = "18";
          els.mpg.value = "18";
        }
      }

      update();
    }

    // Inputs + selects
    app.addEventListener("input", function (e) {
      if (e.target.matches("input, select")) {
        update();
      }
    });

    // Van type -> sync MPG
    if (els.vanType && els.mpg) {
      els.vanType.addEventListener("change", function () {
        els.mpg.value = this.value;
        update();
      });
    }

    // Preset buttons
    presetButtons.forEach(function (btn) {
      btn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        var name = btn.getAttribute("data-vl-preset");

        presetButtons.forEach(function (b) {
          b.classList.toggle("is-active", b === btn);
        });

        applyPreset(name);
      });
    });

    // Initial paint (use current default values)
    update();
  }

  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", initVanlifeTripBudgetApp);
  } else {
    initVanlifeTripBudgetApp();
  }
})();</script>  <script async src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-5665424979389361&amp;host=ca-host-pub-2644536267352236" crossorigin="anonymous"></script> <link rel="preload" href="https://mellownomadic.com/wp-content/fonts/bebas-neue/JTUSjIg69CK48gW7PXoo9Wlhyw.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload" href="https://mellownomadic.com/wp-content/fonts/open-sans/memvYaGs126MiZpBA-UvWbX2vVnXBbObj2OVTS-muw.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link rel="preload" href="https://mellownomadic.com/wp-content/fonts/roboto-slab/BngMUXZYTXPIvIBgJJSb6ufN5qU.woff2" as="font" type="font/woff2" crossorigin><link data-optimized="1" rel='stylesheet' id='kadence-fonts-gfonts-css' href='https://mellownomadic.com/wp-content/litespeed/css/3ca24441a2dc29f559deca39b256225f.css?ver=69084' media='all' /> <script type="application/ld+json" class="kadence-faq-schema-graph kadence-faq-schema-graph--kb-faq3347_52855b-62">{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"FAQPage","mainEntity":[{"@type":"Question","name": "What is the Nomadic Life Starter Kit?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type": "Answer","text": "<p>The Starter Kit is a free, step-by-step resource that helps you plan, prep, and start your van or nomadic life adventure with confidence.</p>"}},{"@type":"Question","name": "Who is this Starter Kit for?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type": "Answer","text": "<p>It’s designed for beginners, weekend travelers, or anyone curious about living on the road — no prior experience needed.</p>"}},{"@type":"Question","name": "Is van life actually safe?","acceptedAnswer":{"@type": "Answer","text": "<p>Yes!
